	xm2_62  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm3_61 + 0.5*xm2_61 + 0.25*xm1_61);
	xm1_62  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm2_61 + 0.5*xm1_61 + 0.25*x0_61);
	x0_62  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm1_61 + 0.5*x0_61 + 0.25*xp1_61);
	xp1_62  rnd64 =   (0.25*x0_61 + 0.5*xp1_61 + 0.25*xp2_61);
	xp2_62  rnd64 =   (0.25*xp1_61 + 0.5*xp2_61 + 0.25*xp3_61);
	xm1_63  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm2_62 + 0.5*xm1_62 + 0.25*x0_62);
	x0_63  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm1_62 + 0.5*x0_62 + 0.25*xp1_62);
	xp1_63  rnd64 =   (0.25*x0_62 + 0.5*xp1_62 + 0.25*xp2_62);
	x0_64  rnd64 =   (0.25*xm1_63 + 0.5*x0_63 + 0.25*xp1_63);

}
